At rest, a human consumes about 250 millilitres of oxygen each minute. With exercise this rate can be increased more than 10-fold in a normal healthy individual, but a highly trained athlete may achieve a more than 20-fold increase..<br />\n<br />\nMuscle can do more work, but beyond the aerobic scope they must revert to anaerobic metabolism, which results in waste products, mainly lactic acid.<br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPS9WtlJfKI/AAAAAAAABKs/PZf4E8Jg82k/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPS9WtlJfKI/AAAAAAAABKs/PZf4E8Jg82k/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nHere is a simple test\u2014fill up a bathtub with slightly hot water\u2014 take a deep breath\u2014 and lie down with your head under water \u2014 you will be up in less than 30 seconds\u2014</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nTry this and get convinced -- It is about the capacity red cells in your blood to absorbing more oxygen from the air breathed into the lungs<br />\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPTAHpks4lI/AAAAAAAABLE/PLKtLLhiP4M/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPTAHpks4lI/AAAAAAAABLE/PLKtLLhiP4M/s320/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" width=\"237\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nDavid Blain held his breath for 17 minutes and 4 seconds in a Oprah Winfey\u2019s show. The main purpose of respiration is to provide oxygen to the cells at a rate adequate to satisfy their metabolic needs. This involves transport of oxygen from the lung to the tissues by means of the circulation of blood. The precise object of respiration therefore is the supply of oxygen to the mitochondria.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nGanges' self-purifying quality leads to oxygen levels 25 times higher than any other river in the world. <span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">she was bald too with &nbsp;a small pox scarred face smoothened with cosmetics , though her portraits were of a beautiful lady</span> ).</span><br increase the wealth of England.. Her drug cartel agent in India was David Sassoon. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">She was also the first African Slave trader who encouraged her pet &nbsp;slave trader Jack Hawkins . She knighted both Jack Hawkins and the son of David , Albert Sassoon for toeing her line. Sir Albert Sassoon married Aline Caroline Rothschild --the first drug cartel family.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">Queen Elizabeth 1 , by her own admission bathed only 4 times in a year \" whether I needed it or not!\" ( while actually she bathed only twice as she did NOT want to remove the white lead compound filling up the small pox pits on her face)</span>.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">But she had more than 2000 of those funny extravagant dresses with hilarious frilled collars</span>. &nbsp;The whole idea was to distract attention from her repulsive ugliness--one way or the other-- including a jarring red coloured wig. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"> </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">She filled up the hideous deep pox pits on her face, using a compound including white lead, which ate away her skin. &nbsp;She died a virgin ,and hence is called the \"Virgin Queen\". There was no way even a ugly common man would have been sexually aroused by her.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-B0lJNZ_XYIo/TWhPSBg-BJI/AAAAAAAADsM/CQjJ5mhSqAo/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-B0lJNZ_XYIo/TWhPSBg-BJI/AAAAAAAADsM/CQjJ5mhSqAo/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Elizabeth 1 proved to be more diabolical than her half sister , Bloody Mary</span>. She had Mary Stuart, the Queen of Scots executed. Though she signed her death warrant, Elizabeth 1 ,did NOT want it to be known to the public. </i></span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i>The Queen of Scots Mary Stuart , was a very pretty, sensuous, and tall woman, and it is speculated, that it was sheer female jealously , which made Elizabeth imprison her for 19 years, and then execute her ( not fear of losing her throne to her, as many considered that she was the true heir ) .&nbsp;</i></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-EgigTZgsr_8/TWhOVN4C1BI/AAAAAAAADsE/dYB7eOaG2oc/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-EgigTZgsr_8/TWhOVN4C1BI/AAAAAAAADsE/dYB7eOaG2oc/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">She was publicly disrobed in disgrace, by several men, the executioner took three strokes with his axe to behead her, with lot of time in between the strokes. Then her decapitated head was held &nbsp;high by the auburn hair, to show the public, with the executioner shouting , as he was told to \" God, save the Queen\". . </span></i></span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">The head fell down , and it turned out to be a wig, with very short grey hair underneath, -- the final cruel blow, even after death..- All engineered by bald and pox scarred faced Elizabeth 1.</span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/-S4FXUT89NDA/TWhOfVVj3iI/AAAAAAAADsI/BT_zjxTb2b0/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/-S4FXUT89NDA/TWhOfVVj3iI/AAAAAAAADsI/BT_zjxTb2b0/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">And then the most bizarre thing was her tiny dog, kept hidden under her petty coat (</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\"> insinuating that this poor dog was always at her crotch </span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">) &nbsp;, was let loose, totally covered in blood- with the desperate creature yelping most pitiably, running helter skelter.</span></span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 15.75pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; His sick room was filled with a nauseating, terrible stench . <span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">&nbsp;</span></span></span><span style=\"line-height: 20px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TOu78Vgd41I/AAAAAAAAAoE/eY59ZQaLUjE/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TOu78Vgd41I/AAAAAAAAAoE/eY59ZQaLUjE/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/S-heaFLp2nI/AAAAAAAAAVQ/C_C4Bsf6RKY/s1600/HM.jpg\" onblur=\"try {parent.deselectBloggerImageGracefully();} catch(e) {}\"><img alt=\"\" border=\"0\" id=\"BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5469725549602134642\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/S-heaFLp2nI/AAAAAAAAAVQ/C_C4Bsf6RKY/s320/HM.jpg\" style=\"float: left; height: 120px; margin: 0px 10px 10px 0px; width: 123px;\" /></a><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nHUMOR MANAGEMENT: by CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO_mN-NlhMI/AAAAAAAAAzs/reC3nS7mL2g/s1600/imagesCAX064Y1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO_mN-NlhMI/AAAAAAAAAzs/reC3nS7mL2g/s1600/imagesCAX064Y1.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nIN MY VISION FOR THE NEXT CENTURY----NO MANAGER WITH GET A JOB PURELY ON IQ ( INTELLIGENCE QUOTIENT ) OR EQ ( EMOTIONAL QUOTIENT ) MERITS. WITHOUT PROVEN HQ ( HUMOR QUOTIENT ) HE WILL NOT GET HIRED.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nNobody will be stupid enough to confuse dour seriousness ---probably related to piles , peptic ulcer or pure misanthropy , with professionalism.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nRather HQ will be taken as an indicator of freedom of human spirit which is required of a leader of men. And a wise man once spake---if you must rule the world--- first keep it amused. ( a small bird told me this, tee heee!!)<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPI7sN5aikI/AAAAAAAABBc/SF1owCLgpVM/s1600/imagesCADR37Z3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPI7sN5aikI/AAAAAAAABBc/SF1owCLgpVM/s1600/imagesCADR37Z3.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<br />\nWhat all powerful and magical HQ can be used for ---<br />\n<br />\nTo tune the reception antenna of others. Any idiot can get the attention of others very few can hold their interest.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo disarm anger. Humor does not appeal to the sense of logic. It appeals to the sense of enjoyment .<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo manage conflict \u2013go for the jocular vein! ( well it is somewhere near the jugular vein ) Use positive empathetic humor instead of counter attacks to defuse resistance<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo manage stress and put people at ease. Ever heard of endorphins released by the brain? Well its is something like morphine only difference being it is a natural chemical triggered by the level of catecholamines in the blood.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nNobody enjoys all aspects of a job on a chemical tanker. But looking at the funny side can keep the tough parts palatable.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo have fun on the job\u2014it is no crime at all to put joy back into work. Crew on a happy ship will have a spring in their step. ( no wending weary ways around)<br />\n<br />\nTo get results on the job ---and surely it is contagious.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo make it hard for people to stay mad at you--- when you have darted to and fro from iron fisted no nonsense management.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo laugh at yourself before anybody else can when you have goofed up..<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo use as a social lubricant ( well don\u2019t think about KY jelly ) it helps build quality relationships.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo improve morale and team cooperation.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo persuade and encourage. For humor is not totalitarian rather it is democratic.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo develop flexible thinking<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo promote innovation. By making it legitimate to think in strange and seemingly illogical ways. Remember the mark of a genius is not perfection but originality.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo encourage novel approaches and perspectives.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPI70f1AkZI/AAAAAAAABBg/6dkTpsLBFqY/s1600/imagesCAN7D81V.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPI70f1AkZI/AAAAAAAABBg/6dkTpsLBFqY/s1600/imagesCAN7D81V.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nWhat it should not be used for\u2014<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo deflect valid criticism<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo detract from a serious discussion<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo be sarcastic \u2013very strong human bonds where you take each other for granted cannot be damaged by sarcasm. Offended listeners seldom appreciate good ideas.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo be funny using ethnic humor .--- Idea is to laugh with people , not at them.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo hide behind humor ( you cant solve problems this way )<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTo misrepresent--- remember there is zilch justification in this. Once you are dog tagged as an ace bullshitter ,remember you lose trust. Crewing managers beware.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nSo then let me think about a couple of times I used humor myself just to justify all my words above.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\na)At school I was participating in an elocution contest. A girl ( all pretty girls were my sworn enemies as I often did a Salman Khan on them\u2014fingering only, of the abstract type ) heckled and I went blank. I lunged into my pocket for the speech got a quick handle of it and then declared with an offended look. My notes say that at this very point I must pause for 30 seconds for audience applause before I continue. I got terrific applause from jury too , continued with aplomb and got the prize.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nb)At Quinghaung dao my ship got caught for pollution ( e room rags ) in 1987. A tug with about 12 people including the agent came to anchorage at 0600 in the morning. A fine of 10 grand USD was made . Just as the party was about to get off , I sort of identified the number one man ( political power ) took him to the alleyway along with the agent and declared \u201c you cant do this to me\u201d. He asked me \u201cwhy not?\u201d I pleaded to his sense of logic \u201c because both of us got a black mole on the same place, and I tapped both our noses\u201d . He burst into laughter and to my great relief tore up the fine voucher then and there. The penavico agent said he has never seen anything like this before. Later both chief officer and chief engineer wanted to know how much bribe I paid.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nHumour is a core value of many companies.<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPI76UV9V6I/AAAAAAAABBk/39dsJOqUh5A/s1600/imagesCAK1UICC.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPI76UV9V6I/AAAAAAAABBk/39dsJOqUh5A/s1600/imagesCAK1UICC.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<br />\nHumor comes from the RH side of your brain\u2014which holds the subconscious and your creative side . Keeping yourself at a fun level\u2014helps you to dip easily into the creative side. These are untold secrets of winners , -- on how to play a bad hand well .<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nOur own Lalu Prasad Yadav knows how to do it. When he is being funny , it is just that he is now dipping into the RH side.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nLaughter releases chemicals and returns the body to a state of balance. Make an effort to be humorous throughout the day. Smile often, laugh often, know 3 great jokes. When you say goodbye have a good parting joke. Laughter is extra ordinarily liberating as well as healing.<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPI8Ezaa05I/AAAAAAAABBo/X5Ky6riHr2U/s1600/imagesCAW77T28.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPI8Ezaa05I/AAAAAAAABBo/X5Ky6riHr2U/s1600/imagesCAW77T28.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<br />\nShared laughter creates a bond of friendships. When people laugh together, they cease to be young and old , big and small, man and woman . Laughter is the shortest distance between human hearts .<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nHumor is just another defense against the universe. Laughter increases the number of neuropeptides that facilitate communication between cells and the nervous system. It stimulates electrical impulses in all parts of the brain, which in turn increases positive energy , reduces stress , increases your serotin levels and a sense of well being. Laughter comes from the center of our being, from the core of our heart<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nLasting happiness comes from accumulation of unforgettable moments . These moments must be mostly moments of achievement while you had fun, and from great friendships The fastest way to improve relationships is to make the other feel important in every way possible.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nMake the first and last minute count in a meeting. Remember names. It is the sweetest sound people know. Get wildly interested in what others have to say to you\u2014 they will fall in love with you.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nIn relationships learn to give happiness and love. If you are not in harmony with your fellow beings , or if you are not satisfied you\u2019re your lot , you cannot be happy. In a unhappy state everything gets blown out of proportion, magnifying our concerns.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPI8NXYsMtI/AAAAAAAABBs/5fVGN6dK1ro/s1600/imagesCAZN0GE8.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPI8NXYsMtI/AAAAAAAABBs/5fVGN6dK1ro/s1600/imagesCAZN0GE8.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nTap into moments of joy again and again and absorb them into your present moment. Happy employees can maintain a balance between hard work, dedication, skill and creativity. The key to success is to ride the line between happiness and contentment and to balance satisfaction with aspiration.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 115%;\">May the holes in your net be no larger than the fish in it.</span></i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 115%;\"> <b><i>- Irish Blessing<span style=\"color: red; font-size: 7.5pt;\"></span></i></b></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO_lL4OlWzI/AAAAAAAAAzo/XdEePNtCBxc/s1600/imagesCAH556H1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">YES, &nbsp;MOST OF &nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;\">THE FABULOUSLY RICH BOMBAY PARSIS IN THE 19<sup>TH</sup> CENTURY , WHEN INDIA WAS UNDER THE BRITISH RULE WERE DRUG RUNNERS.</span> &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">THEY HAD THE GOOD SENSE TO INVEST EVERYTHING IN APPRECIATING PRIME LAND THEY SECURED FROM THE GRATEFUL BRITISH --AT THROW AWAY PRICES, AND TO BUILD TIMELESS PHILANTHROPIC INSTITUTIONS. ALL OF THEM HAVE THEIR NAMES ALLOTTED TO PRINCIPAL STREETS OF MUMBAI.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">THESE HONOURABLE FOLKS PAY IT MONEY TO GET RID OF THEIR NAMES OF THEIR FOREFATHERS FROM THE INTERNET, ON&nbsp; A REGULAR BASIS.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">All of them are founders of the HSBC bank in 1865, at Hong Kong. They are also the first FREE MASON lodge members of India.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-kWs7BKw4iNk/TkQGrRqkzgI/AAAAAAAAFRs/_8f4IvvFtVk/s1600/imagesCA9VDYFP.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-kWs7BKw4iNk/TkQGrRqkzgI/AAAAAAAAFRs/_8f4IvvFtVk/s1600/imagesCA9VDYFP.jpg\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">What follows is authentic information dug out from the records of Jardine and Matheson correspondence by letters , and Chinese verbally.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Those days there was NO email or telex. Letters and manifests have to be burnt, if it should not leave a trail.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-RmHkIE4s1AE/TkQGxjjnCfI/AAAAAAAAFRw/LjTO9GgN1u8/s1600/imagesCAXDKN9H.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-RmHkIE4s1AE/TkQGxjjnCfI/AAAAAAAAFRw/LjTO9GgN1u8/s1600/imagesCAXDKN9H.jpg\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The British East India Company in 1750 started cultivating Opium in Bengal and Bihar to finance its own private army of 1.5 lakh soldiers&nbsp; . As a result there were many famines and deaths in India due to lack of food.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">By 1790 they established an monopoly on Opium trade \u2013 and poppy growers in Indian could sell only to the East India Company.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"> </span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-bVCwJZKQT3o/TVQNljVn45I/AAAAAAAADXA/E9WRZ2HGd9s/s1600/images+%252811%2529a.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"292\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-bVCwJZKQT3o/TVQNljVn45I/AAAAAAAADXA/E9WRZ2HGd9s/s400/images+%252811%2529a.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"> </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Th East India company owned by Jews R family was just a front for the Queen. She needed the money to prevent the Empire from becoming bankrupt , as she planned to expand&nbsp; colonial rule.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Britain could no longer afford to buy tea from China in exchange for Silver. Opium was the free and easy option. Thousands of Bengali , Bihari and Malva &nbsp;Indian farmers were forced to grow Opium . </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The British queen Victoria was the biggest drug trafficker in the 19<sup>th</sup> century.&nbsp; Britain made drug&nbsp; addicts out of 10 million Chinese.&nbsp; Opium is highly addictive , and heavy users last just 5 years.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-TCKjT4OBwrc/Vel0cyykLxI/AAAAAAAA8rQ/MUW89jQlOiE/s1600/dowenload.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"336\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-TCKjT4OBwrc/Vel0cyykLxI/AAAAAAAA8rQ/MUW89jQlOiE/s400/dowenload.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It makes a entire race passive , with no will to work. Opium was banned in China since nearly 100 years before this.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-5qJRjY2Gs-w/Vel0jyQMtkI/AAAAAAAA8rY/aLE4sft07js/s1600/18086797561.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"480\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-5qJRjY2Gs-w/Vel0jyQMtkI/AAAAAAAA8rY/aLE4sft07js/s640/18086797561.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It was Warren Hastings , the first Governor General of India\u2019s , idea to first traffic drugs to China in 1780. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Even Queen Victoria used Opium ( Laudanum ) , and records exist in the Royal Apothecary at Balmoral, as to how many times Opium&nbsp; was passed on to the royal palace. Gladstone openly took Laudanum ( opium + alcohol in ratio of 1:12 ). A lot of British noblemen were Opium eaters.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Free Mason Lodges of Britain and USA have their origins in the opium trade, which made them fabulously rich\u2014and they could buy the unlimited power.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">NOW I WILL TALK ABOUT THE INDIAN SCENE.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-38dv-HKjP8o/Vel0qfVLn9I/AAAAAAAA8rg/D0ghCxm3zJ4/s1600/100-year-old-bfritish-india-rare-photos%2B%252893%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"446\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-38dv-HKjP8o/Vel0qfVLn9I/AAAAAAAA8rg/D0ghCxm3zJ4/s640/100-year-old-bfritish-india-rare-photos%2B%252893%2529.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In India too we had a similar power brokers. They were the Parsis who came to India as refugees from Iran ,and till the Opium trade started were petty shop keepers and garbage ( raddhi &nbsp;like empty bottles and papers ) buyers/ sellers.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">These Parsis made fantastic fortunes by being middle men of the British who trusted them , as they were not proper Indians, and had no scruples when it came to prostituting their souls.</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8aqiuOvKO98/Vel0whXbK1I/AAAAAAAA8ro/a-fgJY6l3D4/s1600/oegpe0e10.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8aqiuOvKO98/Vel0whXbK1I/AAAAAAAA8ro/a-fgJY6l3D4/s640/oegpe0e10.jpg\" width=\"508\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In 1857 the British crown orchestrated the Indian Sepoy Mutiny or The first war of Independence, by provoking the superstitious &nbsp;Indian with pig and cow lard. After that the British Empire under Lord Palmerston just took over India\u2014they did NOT require a front like East India company with a private army any more. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"> </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">And Queen Victoria officially became empress of India.. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Opium trade in India was controlled by the Parsis . &nbsp;Some of them also started the Indigenous shipping and the Wadia Mazagaon /Sassoon docks.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"> </span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-6--oL_HHlHw/TVQoPau8dFI/AAAAAAAADXY/KDoY-2Ellas/s1600/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-6--oL_HHlHw/TVQoPau8dFI/AAAAAAAADXY/KDoY-2Ellas/s400/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" width=\"219\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"> </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The King pin of the Parsi lot was JJ or Sir J#msedjee Jeejee#hoy ( 1753 to 1859 ). He shared his spoils with the British , was their middle-man, and did their dirty work\u2014so they knighted him in 1842 \u2013and made him a Baron in 1857.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">He partnered Jardine and Matheson in HongKong to be the leaders of the biggest drug cartel in the world. He was &nbsp;one of the 6 directors of the Bank of Bombay, in addition to owning ships, agencies, brokering houses, &nbsp;and commercial clearing houses.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">JJ was born in India in 1783, to a impoverished weaver in Yatha Yahu Vairyo Muhalla near Crawford market Mumbai. --and soon became an orphan. &nbsp; Till the age of 16 he had NO formal education. Then he burst into the big league of drug running. He visited China on East India company ships. &nbsp;He was also called Battliwala, as he lived with his uncle Framjee who dealt in recycled garbage bottles &nbsp;.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">At the age of 20 he married Batliwala\u2019s 10 year old daughter Avibhai.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">He was the first to be knighted from India and made a Baron, by a grateful queen Victoria\u2014as he held the moolah.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">JJ was initiated into the opium trade by another Parsi by the name of Hirji Readymoney. Hirji has small ships smuggling opium to Canton in 1755. &nbsp;His sudden wealth and splurge earned him the nickname Ready money.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kG0pcp8URtI/Vel07Lwzs0I/AAAAAAAA8rw/a7UQ_pRDWE0/s1600/100-year-old-british-infdia-rare-photos%2B%252869%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"468\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kG0pcp8URtI/Vel07Lwzs0I/AAAAAAAA8rw/a7UQ_pRDWE0/s640/100-year-old-british-infdia-rare-photos%2B%252869%2529.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Soon P#stonji Boma#ji Wa#ia from Parel , C#wasji, P#tit, Patel, Mehta , Modi, Cama ,Ta#a etc joined them . &nbsp;Wa#ia built the Cusrow baug, Lal Baug, Navroz baug and Ness baug.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">See \"freedom fighter\" Madame Cama below. Her lawyer husband Rustom Cama and her Patel parents were in the drug business.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-BhVxq6lgIr8/Tnt1IqF2YBI/AAAAAAAAGYc/oDq_KBNVTBE/s1600/madame+cama.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-BhVxq6lgIr8/Tnt1IqF2YBI/AAAAAAAAGYc/oDq_KBNVTBE/s320/madame+cama.jpg\" width=\"205\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">JJ made several trips to Canton by ship , with his chinese servants. He became close friends with Jardine in 1805 on a trip to China. &nbsp;Parsis monopolized the Malva opium. On one of his trips he met Matheson who was being held captive by the French in China.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In 1859 Nussarwanji Tata floated the firm Jamsetji and Ardeshir in Hong Kong with two other partners to import opium.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-b9Vbs5EPEFg/Vel1A-rpynI/AAAAAAAA8r4/D1MxHx63wWc/s1600/oegpee008.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"562\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-b9Vbs5EPEFg/Vel1A-rpynI/AAAAAAAA8r4/D1MxHx63wWc/s640/oegpee008.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A Bagdadhi jew by the name of Sassoon (blood relative of Rothschild family ) gave the Parsis stiff competition in the drug trade. He built Sassoon docks, Elphinstone college, Sassoon library &nbsp;and Flora fountain.&nbsp; </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-hUFeL9Lw6sA/Vel1GIN6FNI/AAAAAAAA8sA/fQnsVaZx5Ao/s1600/oegpe0e09.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"526\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-hUFeL9Lw6sA/Vel1GIN6FNI/AAAAAAAA8sA/fQnsVaZx5Ao/s640/oegpe0e09.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">One of our Ex- Naval Chief of Staff Admiral Samson is a Bagdhadi jew. By 1860 Sassoon left the Parsis behind as the Rothschild Jews favoured another blood relative Jew for the secretive and cut throat Opium trade, &nbsp;rather than Ex-Persians. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-W4nJ3vQtSHw/TVQNORydgZI/AAAAAAAADW8/7XYCL_5VTAY/s1600/images+%252829%2529+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-W4nJ3vQtSHw/TVQNORydgZI/AAAAAAAADW8/7XYCL_5VTAY/s400/images+%252829%2529+%25281%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> <span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"> </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The first Opium war started because Sassoons opium was confiscated by the Chinese emperor. An outraged Sassoon had the clout and the arm twisting ability &nbsp;to force the Queen to battle for him. She was on the Shanghai tea run.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"> </span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both;
